# Encounters for PFS Scenario #7-05: Battle of the Thorns

All Distinct Stat BlocksLevels 9-10Levels 11-12Challenge PointsDisplay in columnsPrint in columnsJustify text when printing50% font size when printing60% font size when printing70% font size when printing80% font size when printing90% font size when printing100% font size when printingPrint

## Encounter A1 (Levels 9-10)

### [Greater Hell Hound](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=3048.md)Creature 9

Large [Beast](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=547.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 194](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 26 &bull; Beast ([Arcana](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=35.md), [Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md)), Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +19; [darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md), [scent](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=74.md) ([imprecise](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2407&Redirected=1.md)) 120 feet
Languages [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md); (can't speak any language)
Skills [Acrobatics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=34&Redirected=1.md) +18, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36&Redirected=1.md) +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18, Survival +20 (+22 to [Track](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2408.md))
Str +6, Dex +5, Con +5, Int -2, Wis +4, Cha -2

---

AC 28; Fort +21, Ref +19, Will +16
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md); Weaknesses [cold](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=555.md) 10
Hellish Revenge [reaction] Trigger The greater hell hound is critically hit by any Strike; Effect The greater hell hound's Hellfire Breath recharges. They can immediately use it as part of this reaction.

---

Speed 40 feet
Melee [one-action] jaws +21 [+16/+11] (magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 2d8+9 piercing plus 2d6 fireHellfire Breath [one-action] (divine, fire, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The hell hound breathes flames that deal 10d6 fire damage to all creatures in a 15-foot cone (DC 28 basic Reflex save.) The hell hound can't use Hellfire Breath again for 1d4 rounds. If the greater hell hound would take fire damage or be targeted by a [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) effect, their Hellfire Breath recharges.Pack Attack The greater hell hound's Strikes deal 1d8 extra damage to creatures within the reach of at least two of their allies.

### [Vordine](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2906.md)Creature 5

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 87](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 20 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +12; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md); telepathy 100 feet
Skills [Acrobatics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=34&Redirected=1.md) +13, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36&Redirected=1.md) +15, Intimidation +13, Religion +12, Warfare Lore +13
Str +4, Dex +4, Con +5, Int +2, Wis +3, Cha +2
Items breastplate, trident, whip

---

AC 22; Fort +14, Ref +13, Will +10; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 60; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md); Resistances physical 5 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 5; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 5
[Reactive Strike](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=48.md) [reaction]

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] trident +15 [+10/+5] (magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 1d8+10 piercingMelee [one-action] hoof +15 [+11/+7] (agile, magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 1d4+7 bludgeoning plus 1d4 fireMelee [one-action] whip +15 [+10/+5] ([unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md), [disarm](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=577.md), [magical](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md), [nonlethal](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=661.md), [reach 10 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=684.md), [trip](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=716.md)), Damage 1d4+10 bludgeoningRanged [one-action] trident +13 [+8/+3] (magical, thrown 20 feet, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 1d8+10 piercingDivine Innate Spells DC 19; 4th [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will)
Rituals DC 19; 1st diabolic pact
Burning Hoofprints [two-actions] (divine, fire, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The vordine Strides, trailing hoofprints in each square they exit. The hoofprints burn for 1 minute. A creature on the ground that enters a square with burning hoofprints or begins its turn in one takes 1d4 fire damage.Trident of Dis [one-action] The vordine makes a trident Strike, increasing their reach to 10 feet for that Strike. If there is an [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md) ally between the vordine and their target, that creature's energy causes the Strike to deal an additional 1d6 spirit damage.

### [Warden](../NPC/NPCs.aspx-ID=3562.md)Creature 6

Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 117
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 22 &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +17
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md)
Skills [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +15, [Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md) +11, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48.md) +13, [Survival](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=49.md) +13
Str +4, Dex +2, Con +3, Int +1, Wis +2, Cha +1
Items +1 [composite longbow](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=434.md) (10 arrows), backpack, bastard sword, bedroll, compass, flint and steel, maps, pup tent, scale mail

---

AC 24; Fort +15, Ref +15, Will +11
HP 100
Warding Strike [reaction] Trigger One of the warden's enemies within 100 feet attacks one of the warden's allies or a person the warden is sworn to protect; Effect The warden Strikes the triggering enemy. If the Strike hits, the enemy's attack is deflected, reducing its damage by 8, or by 16 if the warden's Strike was a critical hit.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] bastard sword +16 [+11/+6] (two-hand d12), Damage 1d8+10 slashingMelee [one-action] fist +16 [+12/+8] (agile, nonlethal, unarmed), Damage 1d4+10 bludgeoningRanged [one-action] composite longbow +17 [+12/+7] (deadly d10, magical, propulsive, [range increment 100 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=248.md), [reload 0](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=254.md), volley 30 feet), Damage 1d8+8 piercingWarden's Protection A warden deals an extra 1d8 damage to any creature trespassing on the territory the warden protects.

### GendarmeCreature 8

Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 117
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 24 &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +19
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md)
Skills [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +18, [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) +16, [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +14
Str +4, Dex +1, Con +4, Int +0, Wis +3, Cha +2
Items +1 [gauntlet](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=359.md), +1 [striking](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2829.md) [flail](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=374.md), +1 [composite longbow](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=434.md) (20 arrows), half plate

---

AC 26; Fort +19, Ref +14, Will +17 (nerves of steel)
HP 120
Nerves of Steel When the gendarme succeeds against a fear effect, they get a critical success instead.[Reactive Strike](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=48.md) [reaction] The gendarme can [Disarm](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2383.md) instead of Striking.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] flail +19 [+14/+9] (disarm, magical, sweep, trip), Damage 2d6+10 bludgeoning plus Improved KnockdownMelee [one-action] gauntlet +19 [+15/+11] (agile, free-hand, magical), Damage 1d4+10 bludgeoning plus Improved GrabRanged [one-action] composite longbow +16 [+11/+6] (deadly d10, magical, propulsive, [range increment 100 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=248.md), volley 30 feet), Damage 1d8+8 piercingStop in the Name of the Law! [two-actions] (incapacitation, linguistic) The gendarme Strides twice and then [Demoralizes](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2395.md). On a success, the target is [slowed](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=92.md) with a value equal to its [frightened](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md) value until it is no longer frightened.Shoot Down [two-actions] The gendarme carefully makes a ranged Strike. If the Strike deals damage, the target must succeed at a DC 26 Reflex saving throw or fall [prone](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=88.md).

## Encounter A1 (Levels 9-10; 12-13 Challenge Points)

### [Greater Hell Hound](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=3048.md)Creature 9

Large [Beast](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=547.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 194](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 26 &bull; Beast ([Arcana](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=35.md), [Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md)), Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))

---

The hell hound can't use Hellfire Breath again for 1d4 rounds. If the greater hell hound would take fire damage or be targeted by a [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) effect, their Hellfire Breath recharges.Pack Attack The greater hell hound's Strikes deal 1d8 extra damage to creatures within the reach of at least two of their allies.

---

Rituals DC 25; 1st diabolic pact
Despairing Shriek [two-actions] (divine, sonic, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The coarti lets out a terrible cry, dealing 4d6 sonic damage to all creatures in a 30-foot emanation with a DC 25 basic Will save. [Holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) creatures that fail this save are also [frightened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md); this added effect has the [emotion](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=590.md), [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md), and [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) traits. The coarti can't use Despairing Shriek again for 1d4 rounds.Wing Snap [one-action] Frequency once per turn; Effect The coarti makes two wing Strikes, then falls if it's flying. It can't Fly until the end of its turn.

Melee [one-action] morningstar +18 [+13/+8] (magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md), versatile P), Damage 1d6+10 bludgeoning plus 1d6 spiritMelee [one-action] wing +17 [+13/+9] (agile, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md), versatile P), Damage 1d6+7 bludgeoning plus 1d6 fireDivine Innate Spells DC 25; 4th darkness, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 25; 1st diabolic pact
Despairing Shriek [two-actions] (divine, sonic, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The coarti lets out a terrible cry, dealing 4d6 sonic damage to all creatures in a 30-foot emanation with a DC 25 basic Will save. [Holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) creatures that fail this save are also [frightened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md); this added effect has the [emotion](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=590.md), [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md), and [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) traits. The coarti can't use Despairing Shriek again for 1d4 rounds.Wing Snap [one-action] Frequency once per turn; Effect The coarti makes two wing Strikes, then falls if it's flying. It can't Fly until the end of its turn.

## Encounter A2 (Levels 9-10; 12-13 Challenge Points)

### Drill SergeantCreature 8

Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 93
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 24 &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +16
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md)
Skills [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +18, [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) +20, [Warfare Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +18
Str +4, Dex +3, Con +2, Int +2, Wis +2, Cha +4
Items +1 [striking](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2829.md) [longsword](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=386.md), chain shirt, javelin (6)

---

AC 25; Fort +14, Ref +15, Will +20
HP 120
Commanding Aura ([aura](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=542.md), [emotion](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=590.md), [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md), [visual](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=727.md)) 60 feet. An ally that starts its turn in the aura gains 8 temporary Hit Points. These last until the start of the creature's next turn.You Don't Have My Permission to Die! [reaction] ([auditory](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=541.md), [emotion](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=590.md), [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md), [linguistic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=642.md), [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md)) Trigger An allied creature within 30 feet would be reduced to 0 Hit Points; Effect With a stern rebuke, the drill sergeant berates the target for their failure. The creature avoids being [knocked out](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=95.md) and remains at 1 HP. The creature is then temporarily immune for 24 hours.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] longsword +21 [+16/+11] (magical, versatile P), Damage 2d8+12 slashingMelee [one-action] fist +20 [+16/+12] (agile, nonlethal, unarmed), Damage 1d4+12 bludgeoningRanged [one-action] javelin +19 [+14/+9] (thrown 30 feet), Damage 1d6+12 piercingChastising Enforcement [one-action] ([auditory](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=541&Redirected=1.md), emotion, linguistic, mental) The drill sergeant exhorts a faltering comrade with a stern word and attempts an [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) check against the Will DC of one ally within 30 feet. On a success, the target's [frightened](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md) condition is reduced by 2 and the drill sergeant can attempt to counteract one [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effect that ally is suffering from with a +18 counteract modifier. On a critical success, the drill sergeant also reduces the frightened condition of each other ally in a 10-foot emanation around the target by 1.Keep Up With Me! [one-action] ([auditory](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=541&Redirected=1.md), emotion, linguistic, mental) Requirements The drill sergeant's last action was a Strike that hit; Effect The drill sergeant shouts that one ally within 30 feet can't keep up with them. That ally gains a +3 status bonus to their attack roll on the next Strike they make before the start of the drill sergeant's next turn. If the ally is a troop, this bonus instead applies to the DC of their next offensive activity (such as Join the Fray for heavy cavalry).

Rituals DC 19; 1st diabolic pact
Burning Hoofprints [two-actions] (divine, fire, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The vordine Strides, trailing hoofprints in each square they exit. The hoofprints burn for 1 minute. A creature on the ground that enters a square with burning hoofprints or begins its turn in one takes 1d4 fire damage.Trident of Dis [one-action] The vordine makes a trident Strike, increasing their reach to 10 feet for that Strike. If there is an [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md) ally between the vordine and their target, that creature's energy causes the Strike to deal an additional 1d6 spirit damage.

The coarti can't use Despairing Shriek again for 1d4 rounds.Wing Snap [one-action] Frequency once per turn; Effect The coarti makes two wing Strikes, then falls if it's flying. It can't Fly until the end of its turn.

### [Phistophilus](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2909.md)Creature 10

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 90](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 27 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +21; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Aklo](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=13.md), [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md), [Draconic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=2.md), [Empyrean](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=115.md), [Sakvroth](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=118.md); telepathy 100 feet, [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Skills Arcana +19, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +19, [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38&Redirected=1.md) +23, Diplomacy +21, Intimidation +21, Legal Lore +25, Religion +19, Society +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18
Str +3, Dex +4, Con +4, Int +7, Wis +5, Cha +5

---

AC 30; Fort +18, Ref +18, Will +23; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md), ward contract; Resistances physical 10 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 10; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 10
Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

### Weak Line InfantryCreature 5

Gargantuan [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md) Troop
Source NPC Core pg. 90
[Weak](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=3359.md) Changes are marked. The -2 damage penalty to non-strike offensive abilities (-4 if the ability is limited, such as spells) is NOT factored in.
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 20 &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +11
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md)
Skills [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +13, [Warfare Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +10
Str +5, Dex +2, Con +3, Int +0, Wis +1, Cha +0

---

AC 22; Fort +13, Ref +12, Will +11
HP 76 (4 segments); Thresholds 64 (3 segments), 32 (2 segments); Weaknesses area damage 5, [splash](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=699.md) damage 5
No Retreat These soldiers have been extensively trained to hold their ground no matter the situation. If any effect would force the line infantry to move, reduce the distance by 5 feet. Any time they would be affected by the [fleeing](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=74.md) condition, the line infantry is instead [slowed 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=92.md) for the same duration.Troop Defenses

---

Speed 20 feet; troop movement
Bolt Salvo [three-actions] The line infantry draws, loads, and shoots a salvo from their crossbows. The salvo is a 10-foot burst within 120 feet that deals 2d8 piercing damage (DC 19 basic Reflex save). When the line infantry is reduced to 2 or fewer segments, this area decreases to a 5-foot burst.Clash of Steel [one-action] to [three-actions] Frequency once per round; Effect The line infantry lays into each enemy in a 5-foot emanation, with a DC 19 basic Reflex save. The damage depends on the number of actions.
[one-action] 1d6+2 slashing damage
[two-actions] 2d6+7 slashing damage
[three-actions] 3d6+10 slashing damageDrilled in Formations [one-action] Frequency once per round; Effect The line infantry uses Change Formation (see below in Military). A line infantry unit typically knows the marching column and wedge formations.

### GendarmeCreature 8

Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 117
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 24 &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +19
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md)
Skills [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +18, [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) +16, [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +14
Str +4, Dex +1, Con +4, Int +0, Wis +3, Cha +2
Items +1 [gauntlet](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=359.md), +1 [striking](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2829.md) [flail](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=374.md), +1 [composite longbow](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=434.md) (20 arrows), half plate

---

AC 26; Fort +19, Ref +14, Will +17 (nerves of steel)
HP 120
Nerves of Steel When the gendarme succeeds against a fear effect, they get a critical success instead.[Reactive Strike](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=48.md) [reaction] The gendarme can [Disarm](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2383.md) instead of Striking.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] flail +19 [+14/+9] (disarm, magical, sweep, trip), Damage 2d6+10 bludgeoning plus Improved KnockdownMelee [one-action] gauntlet +19 [+15/+11] (agile, free-hand, magical), Damage 1d4+10 bludgeoning plus Improved GrabRanged [one-action] composite longbow +16 [+11/+6] (deadly d10, magical, propulsive, [range increment 100 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=248.md), volley 30 feet), Damage 1d8+8 piercingStop in the Name of the Law! [two-actions] (incapacitation, linguistic) The gendarme Strides twice and then [Demoralizes](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2395.md). On a success, the target is [slowed](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=92.md) with a value equal to its [frightened](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md) value until it is no longer frightened.Shoot Down [two-actions] The gendarme carefully makes a ranged Strike. If the Strike deals damage, the target must succeed at a DC 26 Reflex saving throw or fall [prone](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=88.md).

## Encounter B (Levels 9-10; 12-13 Challenge Points)

### [Hellknight Cavalry Brigade](../NPC/NPCs.aspx-ID=3530.md)Creature 8

Gargantuan [Animal](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=531.md) [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md) Troop
Source NPC Core pg. 93
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 24 &bull; Animal ([Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md)), Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +16
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md)
Skills [Acrobatics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=34.md) +13, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +18, [Hell Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +12, [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) +17, [Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md) +12, [Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md) +12
Str +7, Dex +1, Con +4, Int +2, Wis +2, Cha +3

---

AC 27; Fort +18, Ref +13, Will +16
HP 135 (4 segments); Thresholds 90 (3 segments), 45 (2 segments); Resistances [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) 5, slashing 5; Weaknesses area damage 8, [splash](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=699.md) damage 8
Mounted Troop Effects that target only [animals](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=531.md) or only [humanoids](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md) might not work on the Hellknight cavalry brigade, subject to the GM's discretion.Troop Defenses

---

Speed 40 feet; trailblazing stride, troop movement
Arrow Volley [two-actions] The Hellknights draw or reload their longbows, then launch a ranged attack in the form of a volley. This volley is a 10-foot burst within 100 feet that deals 3d8 piercing damage (DC 23 basic Reflex save). When the troop is reduced to 2 or fewer segments, this area decreases to a 5-foot burst.Lance Charge [three-actions] The brigade Strides twice with a +10-foot circumstance bonus to its Speed. If it moves at least 10 feet, the brigade deals 3d8+14 piercing damage with a DC 26 basic Reflex save to each enemy in a 10-foot emanation at the end of its movement.Stab from the Saddle [one-action] to [three-actions] Frequency once per round; Effect The brigade engages in a coordinated lance attack against each enemy in a 10-foot emanation with a DC 23 basic Reflex save. The damage depends on the number of actions.
[one-action] 1d6+3 piercing damage
[two-actions] 2d6+10 piercing damage
[three-actions] 3d6+14 piercing damageTrailblazing Stride While moving on land, the Hellknight cavalry brigade ignores [difficult terrain](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2366&Redirected=1.md).

### [Phistophilus (2)](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2909.md)Creature 10

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 90](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 27 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +21; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Aklo](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=13.md), [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md), [Draconic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=2.md), [Empyrean](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=115.md), [Sakvroth](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=118.md); telepathy 100 feet, [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Skills Arcana +19, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +19, [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38&Redirected=1.md) +23, Diplomacy +21, Intimidation +21, Legal Lore +25, Religion +19, Society +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18
Str +3, Dex +4, Con +4, Int +7, Wis +5, Cha +5

---

AC 30; Fort +18, Ref +18, Will +23; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md), ward contract; Resistances physical 10 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 10; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 10
Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

The hell hound can't use Hellfire Breath again for 1d4 rounds. If the greater hell hound would take fire damage or be targeted by a [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) effect, their Hellfire Breath recharges.Pack Attack The greater hell hound's Strikes deal 1d8 extra damage to creatures within the reach of at least two of their allies.

The hell hound can't use Hellfire Breath again for 1d4 rounds. ### [Phistophilus](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2909.md)Creature 10

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 90](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 27 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +21; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Aklo](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=13.md), [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md), [Draconic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=2.md), [Empyrean](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=115.md), [Sakvroth](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=118.md); telepathy 100 feet, [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Skills Arcana +19, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +19, [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38&Redirected=1.md) +23, Diplomacy +21, Intimidation +21, Legal Lore +25, Religion +19, Society +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18
Str +3, Dex +4, Con +4, Int +7, Wis +5, Cha +5

---

AC 30; Fort +18, Ref +18, Will +23; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md), ward contract; Resistances physical 10 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 10; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 10
Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

The hell hound can't use Hellfire Breath again for 1d4 rounds. If the greater hell hound would take fire damage or be targeted by a [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) effect, their Hellfire Breath recharges.Pack Attack The greater hell hound's Strikes deal 1d8 extra damage to creatures within the reach of at least two of their allies.

### [Phistophilus (2)](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2909.md)Creature 10

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 90](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 27 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +21; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Aklo](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=13.md), [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md), [Draconic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=2.md), [Empyrean](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=115.md), [Sakvroth](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=118.md); telepathy 100 feet, [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Skills Arcana +19, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +19, [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38&Redirected=1.md) +23, Diplomacy +21, Intimidation +21, Legal Lore +25, Religion +19, Society +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18
Str +3, Dex +4, Con +4, Int +7, Wis +5, Cha +5

---

AC 30; Fort +18, Ref +18, Will +23; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md), ward contract; Resistances physical 10 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 10; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 10
Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

### Infernal RegistrarCreature 10

[Rare](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=683.md) Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 119
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 32 (includes +5 from Rare) &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +19; (33 to [Sense Motive](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2302.md))
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md)

Str +2, Dex +2, Con +2, Int +5, Wis +3, Cha +4
Contract Specialist For encounters involving matters of contracts and dealings with [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md), the infernal registrar is an 18th-level challenge.
Death is a Promotion The infernal registrar does not fear death, as they have a signed infernal contract for immediate promotion to a mid-ranked devil upon their soul's arrival in [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md). They're immune to all [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) checks to [Coerce](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2394.md) involving threats of death.
Friends in Low Places Though devils do not respect most mortals, they respect the office of infernal registrar. No creature with the [devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) trait of 18th level or lower will knowingly and willingly attack an infernal registrar.
Technically Correct The infernal registrar uses their [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) modifier on all [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38.md) checks to [Lie](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2389.md).
Items staff of office (functions as +1 [flaming](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2838.md) [striking](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2829.md) [staff](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=367.md))

---

AC 27; Fort +19, Ref +16, Will +33; +2 circumstance to all saves vs. [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md)
HP 180; Resistances [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) 10

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] staff of office +19 [+14/+9] (magical, two-hand d8), Damage 2d4+8 bludgeoning plus 1d6 fireMelee [one-action] fist +18 [+14/+10] (agile, nonlethal, unarmed), Damage 1d4+8 bludgeoningDivine Innate Spells DC 29, attack +21; 5th banishment, [divine immolation](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1496.md), locate; 4th detect scrying, suggestion; 3rd chilling darkness, fear, [ring of truth](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1656.md); 2nd [translate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1723.md) (at will); Cantrips (5th) detect magic, [ignition](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1565.md), read aura
A Favor for a Favor [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar has the authority to make limited infernal contracts with other mortals. They summon a contract with the legal language they desire. Detecting hidden clauses in the contract requires a successful DC 43 [Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md) or a DC 38 [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check. Once signed, the contract vanishes into the infernal filing system in Hell. The infernal registrar cannot grant any boons beyond their own personal power (usually limited to information, advice, or access to elements of the infernal bureaucracy).Request Document [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar makes a request to summon a copy of any infernal contract a specific creature has signed. They must know enough information to specifically identify the individual who signed. The infernal registrar attempts a [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check with a DC equal to a [hard DC of the level of the creature in question](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2627.md). The infernal registrar will never promise a successful use of this ability in the agreements they make. Each agreement is typically for one attempt. Any copy summoned is simply a copy, has no impact on the original contract if destroyed or altered, and will vanish if taken more than 20 feet from the infernal registrar.
Critical Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 10 minutes.
Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 1 hour.
Failure The attempt fails, but the infernal registrar can try again after 24 hours.
Critical Failure The attempt fails, and the infernal registrar can't try again for the named creature for 1 year.

A Favor for a Favor [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar has the authority to make limited infernal contracts with other mortals. They summon a contract with the legal language they desire. Detecting hidden clauses in the contract requires a successful DC 43 [Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md) or a DC 38 [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check. Once signed, the contract vanishes into the infernal filing system in Hell. The infernal registrar cannot grant any boons beyond their own personal power (usually limited to information, advice, or access to elements of the infernal bureaucracy).Request Document [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar makes a request to summon a copy of any infernal contract a specific creature has signed. They must know enough information to specifically identify the individual who signed. The infernal registrar attempts a [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check with a DC equal to a [hard DC of the level of the creature in question](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2627.md). The infernal registrar will never promise a successful use of this ability in the agreements they make. Each agreement is typically for one attempt. Any copy summoned is simply a copy, has no impact on the original contract if destroyed or altered, and will vanish if taken more than 20 feet from the infernal registrar.
Critical Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 10 minutes.
Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 1 hour.
Failure The attempt fails, but the infernal registrar can try again after 24 hours.
Critical Failure The attempt fails, and the infernal registrar can't try again for the named creature for 1 year.

### Coarti (5)Creature 7

HP 110; Immunities fire; Resistances physical 5 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 5; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 5 (see blood contract)
Blood Contract When the coarti takes damage from their holy weakness, blood flows freely from their eyes and the contract carved into their skin. They take 1d6 [persistent bleed damage](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=86&Redirected=1.md) and are [dazzled](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=65.md) as long as the persistent damage continues, but their Despairing Shriek recharges.

Rituals DC 25; 1st diabolic pact
Despairing Shriek [two-actions] (divine, sonic, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The coarti lets out a terrible cry, dealing 4d6 sonic damage to all creatures in a 30-foot emanation with a DC 25 basic Will save. [Holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) creatures that fail this save are also [frightened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=76.md); this added effect has the [emotion](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=590.md), [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md), and [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) traits. The coarti can't use Despairing Shriek again for 1d4 rounds.Wing Snap [one-action] Frequency once per turn; Effect The coarti makes two wing Strikes, then falls if it's flying. It can't Fly until the end of its turn.

Death is a Promotion The infernal registrar does not fear death, as they have a signed infernal contract for immediate promotion to a mid-ranked devil upon their soul's arrival in [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md). They're immune to all [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) checks to [Coerce](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2394.md) involving threats of death.

Technically Correct The infernal registrar uses their [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) modifier on all [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38.md) checks to [Lie](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2389.md).

### Infernal RegistrarCreature 10

[Rare](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=683.md) Medium [Human](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=627.md) [Humanoid](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=628.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source NPC Core pg. 119
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 32 (includes +5 from Rare) &bull; Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))
Perception +19; (33 to [Sense Motive](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2302.md))
Languages [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md)
Skills [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38.md) +22, [Diplomacy](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=39.md) +33, [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +33, [Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md) +30, [Scribe Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) +30, [Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md) +33
Str +2, Dex +2, Con +2, Int +5, Wis +3, Cha +4
Contract Specialist For encounters involving matters of contracts and dealings with [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md), the infernal registrar is an 18th-level challenge.
Death is a Promotion The infernal registrar does not fear death, as they have a signed infernal contract for immediate promotion to a mid-ranked devil upon their soul's arrival in [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md). They're immune to all [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) checks to [Coerce](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2394.md) involving threats of death.
Friends in Low Places Though devils do not respect most mortals, they respect the office of infernal registrar. No creature with the [devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) trait of 18th level or lower will knowingly and willingly attack an infernal registrar.
Technically Correct The infernal registrar uses their [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) modifier on all [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38.md) checks to [Lie](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2389.md).
Items staff of office (functions as +1 [flaming](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2838.md) [striking](../Equipment/Equipment.aspx-ID=2829.md) [staff](../Weapon/Weapons.aspx-ID=367.md))

---

AC 27; Fort +19, Ref +16, Will +33; +2 circumstance to all saves vs. [fear](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=598.md)
HP 180; Resistances [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) 10

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] staff of office +19 [+14/+9] (magical, two-hand d8), Damage 2d4+8 bludgeoning plus 1d6 fireMelee [one-action] fist +18 [+14/+10] (agile, nonlethal, unarmed), Damage 1d4+8 bludgeoningDivine Innate Spells DC 29, attack +21; 5th banishment, [divine immolation](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1496.md), locate; 4th detect scrying, suggestion; 3rd chilling darkness, fear, [ring of truth](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1656.md); 2nd [translate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1723.md) (at will); Cantrips (5th) detect magic, [ignition](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1565.md), read aura
A Favor for a Favor [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar has the authority to make limited infernal contracts with other mortals. They summon a contract with the legal language they desire. Detecting hidden clauses in the contract requires a successful DC 43 [Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md) or a DC 38 [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check. Once signed, the contract vanishes into the infernal filing system in Hell. The infernal registrar cannot grant any boons beyond their own personal power (usually limited to information, advice, or access to elements of the infernal bureaucracy).Request Document [three-actions] ([concentrate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=561&Redirected=1.md), divine) The infernal registrar makes a request to summon a copy of any infernal contract a specific creature has signed. They must know enough information to specifically identify the individual who signed. The infernal registrar attempts a [Legal Lore](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=41.md) check with a DC equal to a [hard DC of the level of the creature in question](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2627.md). The infernal registrar will never promise a successful use of this ability in the agreements they make. Each agreement is typically for one attempt. Any copy summoned is simply a copy, has no impact on the original contract if destroyed or altered, and will vanish if taken more than 20 feet from the infernal registrar.
Critical Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 10 minutes.
Success A copy of the contract appears before the infernal registrar after 1 hour.
Failure The attempt fails, but the infernal registrar can try again after 24 hours.
Critical Failure The attempt fails, and the infernal registrar can't try again for the named creature for 1 year.

[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 23 &bull; Animal ([Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md)), Humanoid ([Society](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=47.md))

[three-actions] 3d6+10 bludgeoning damageThunder of Hooves [one-action] Frequency once per round; Effect The heavy cavalry Strides. At the end of their movement, the cavalry can either attempt an [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) check to [Trip](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2382.md) each adjacent enemy or an [Intimidation](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=40.md) check to [Demoralize](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2395.md) each enemy within 30 feet. Roll only once and compare the result to each enemy's Reflex DC (for Trip) or Will DC (for Demoralize).Trample [three-actions] Medium or smaller, 2d8+7 bludgeoning, DC 22; creatures that fail the save are also knocked [prone](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=88.md).

### [Phistophilus](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=2909.md)Creature 10

Medium [Devil](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=575.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 90](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 27 &bull; Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +21; [greater darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Aklo](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=13.md), [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Common](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=1.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md), [Draconic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=2.md), [Empyrean](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=115.md), [Sakvroth](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=118.md); telepathy 100 feet, [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Skills Arcana +19, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36.md) +19, [Deception](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=38&Redirected=1.md) +23, Diplomacy +21, Intimidation +21, Legal Lore +25, Religion +19, Society +19, [Stealth](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=48&Redirected=1.md) +18
Str +3, Dex +4, Con +4, Int +7, Wis +5, Cha +5

---

AC 30; Fort +18, Ref +18, Will +23; +1 status to all saves vs. [magic](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=644.md)
HP 150; Immunities [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md), ward contract; Resistances physical 10 (except silver), [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md) 10; Weaknesses [holy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=517.md) 10
Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.

---

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

## Encounter B (Levels 11-12; 16-18 Challenge Points)

### [Greater Nightmare](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=3106.md)Creature 11

Huge [Beast](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=547.md) [Fiend](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=600.md) [Unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)
Source [Monster Core pg. 238](../Source/Sources.aspx-ID=221.md)
[Recall Knowledge](../Rules/Rules.aspx-ID=2638.md) DC 28 &bull; Beast ([Arcana](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=35.md), [Nature](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=43.md)), Fiend ([Religion](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=46.md))
Perception +22; [darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Daemonic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=31.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md)
Skills [Acrobatics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=34&Redirected=1.md) +23, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36&Redirected=1.md) +24, Intimidation +22, Survival +20
Str +7, Dex +4, Con +5, Int +2, Wis +5, Cha +3
Smoke ([aura](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=542.md)) 15 feet. The nightmare continually exhales black smoke. Creatures within the aura are [concealed](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=62.md) to those outside it, and creatures outside the aura are concealed to creatures within it. Nightmares and their riders can see through this smoke.
A creature that begins its turn in the area must succeed at a DC 28 Fortitude save or be [sickened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=91.md). It's then temporarily immune to being sickened by the smoke for 1 minute. This is an [inhaled](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=634.md) [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md), and the nightmare and its rider are immune to it.

---

AC 31; Fort +25, Ref +24, Will +21
HP 200; Resistances [fire](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=604.md) 15

---

Speed 60 feet, fly 120 feet
Melee [one-action] jaws +24 [+19/+14] (magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md), [reach 10 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=684.md)), Damage 3d10+13 piercingMelee [one-action] hoof +24 [+20/+16] (agile, fire, magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 2d8+10 bludgeoning plus 2d6 fireDivine Innate Spells DC 30; 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md) (self and rider only)
Flaming Gallop [two-actions] (divine, fire, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The nightmare Strides or [Flies](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2312.md)up to triple its Speed. Its hooves burst with intense flame, dealing 6d6 fire damage with a DC 30 basic Reflex save to each creature other than the nightmare's rider that the nightmare moves adjacent to during its gallop. Each creature can be affected only once during a single use of Flaming Gallop.Trample [three-actions] Large or smaller, hoof, DC 30

Speed 25 feet
Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

## Encounter B (Levels 11-12; 23-27 Challenge Points)

### [Greater Nightmare](../Monster/Monsters.aspx-ID=3106.md)Creature 11

Perception +22; [darkvision](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=59.md)
Languages [Chthonian](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=114.md), [Daemonic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=31.md), [Diabolic](../Language/Languages.aspx-ID=117.md)
Skills [Acrobatics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=34&Redirected=1.md) +23, [Athletics](../Skill/Skills.aspx-ID=36&Redirected=1.md) +24, Intimidation +22, Survival +20
Str +7, Dex +4, Con +5, Int +2, Wis +5, Cha +3
Smoke ([aura](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=542.md)) 15 feet. The nightmare continually exhales black smoke. Creatures within the aura are [concealed](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=62.md) to those outside it, and creatures outside the aura are concealed to creatures within it. Nightmares and their riders can see through this smoke.
A creature that begins its turn in the area must succeed at a DC 28 Fortitude save or be [sickened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=91.md). It's then temporarily immune to being sickened by the smoke for 1 minute. This is an [inhaled](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=634.md) [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md), and the nightmare and its rider are immune to it.

Melee [one-action] jaws +24 [+19/+14] (magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md), [reach 10 feet](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=684.md)), Damage 3d10+13 piercingMelee [one-action] hoof +24 [+20/+16] (agile, fire, magical, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 2d8+10 bludgeoning plus 2d6 fireDivine Innate Spells DC 30; 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md) (self and rider only)
Flaming Gallop [two-actions] (divine, fire, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)) The nightmare Strides or [Flies](../Action/Actions.aspx-ID=2312.md)up to triple its Speed. Its hooves burst with intense flame, dealing 6d6 fire damage with a DC 30 basic Reflex save to each creature other than the nightmare's rider that the nightmare moves adjacent to during its gallop. Melee [one-action] binding contract +23 [+19/+15] (agile, disarm, magical, reach 10 feet, trip, [unholy](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=521.md)), Damage 3d6+11 slashing plus [Grab](../MonsterAbility/MonsterAbilities.aspx-ID=45.md) and infernal woundMelee [one-action] horn +21 [+16/+11] (magical), Damage 3d10+11 piercing plus infernal woundDivine Innate Spells DC 31; 10th scrying (at will; see infernal investment); 7th [interplanar teleport](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1576.md); 5th fireball, illusory scene, lightning bolt, locate (at will), mind probe, sending (at will), [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md); 4th [peaceful bubble](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1624.md), silence, [translocate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1724.md) (at will); 3rd mind reading (at will); Cantrips (7th) detect magic; Constant (5th) [truespeech](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1728.md)
Rituals DC 31; 1st diabolic pact
Draft Contract [three-actions] (divine, [manipulate](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=645&Redirected=1.md)) The contract devil produces an infernal contract for a single living mortal. This contract can grant a wide range of abilities and effects, akin to the power of a [wish](../Ritual/Rituals.aspx-ID=125.md) ritual but fulfilled to the letter by the contract devil. To receive any of those benefits, the mortal must willingly sign its true name to the contract. At that point, the mortal's soul is bound to the contract devil and [Hell](../Plane/Planes.aspx-ID=42.md).

While the contract is in effect, the victim can't be restored to life except by wish or similar magic. If the mortal is restored to life by those means, the contract devil knows which mortal came to life and can locate the creature or creatures who restored the mortal to life for 1 year, gaining the effects of a [locate](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1588.md) spell with unlimited range. Avoiding the terms of an infernal contract is difficult and often dangerous.Infernal Investment A contract devil can cast a 10th-rank innate [scrying](../Spell/Spells.aspx-ID=1662.md) spell at will, but only to target a creature with which they have a contract. The target automatically critically fails its save.Infernal Wound (divine) The wounds from a contract devil's Strikes resist healing. A spellcaster or item attempting to use [healing](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=623.md) magic on a creature suffering first attempts to counteract infernal wound (DC 29). If it is not counteracted, the healing has no effect.

Str +7, Dex +4, Con +5, Int +2, Wis +5, Cha +3
Smoke ([aura](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=542.md)) 15 feet. The nightmare continually exhales black smoke. Creatures within the aura are [concealed](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=62.md) to those outside it, and creatures outside the aura are concealed to creatures within it. Nightmares and their riders can see through this smoke.
A creature that begins its turn in the area must succeed at a DC 28 Fortitude save or be [sickened 2](../Condition/Conditions.aspx-ID=91.md). It's then temporarily immune to being sickened by the smoke for 1 minute. This is an [inhaled](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=634.md) [poison](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=669.md), and the nightmare and its rider are immune to it.

Ward Contract A signed contract carried by a living contract devil (including draped over their horns) is immune to damage from all creatures other than that contract devil. A contract devil is immune to [mental](../Trait/Traits.aspx-ID=647.md) effects that would make them destroy, nullify, or alter a contract.
